== 5. Configuração da Unit e Environment ==
-- ytc-web-backend.service --
FragmentPath: /etc/systemd/system/ytc-web-backend.service
FragmentTimestamp: <desconhecido>
$ systemctl cat ytc-web-backend.service
(returncode=0)
stdout:
# /etc/systemd/system/ytc-web-backend.service
[Unit]
Description=YTC Web Backend (YouTube status API)
After=network.target

[Service]
Type=simple
User=root
Group=root
WorkingDirectory=/opt/ytc-web-service/app
EnvironmentFile=/etc/ytc-web-backend.env
Environment=PYTHONUNBUFFERED=1
Environment=YTC_WEB_BACKEND_HOST=127.0.0.1
Environment=YTC_WEB_BACKEND_PORT=8081
ExecStart=/opt/ytc-web-service/venv/bin/uvicorn app:app --host ${YTC_WEB_BACKEND_HOST} --port ${YTC_WEB_BACKEND_PORT}
Restart=on-failure
RestartSec=5

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target
-- yt-restapi.service --
FragmentPath: /etc/systemd/system/yt-restapi.service
FragmentTimestamp: <desconhecido>
$ systemctl cat yt-restapi.service
(returncode=0)
stdout:
# /etc/systemd/system/yt-restapi.service
[Unit]
Description=BWB Status Monitor (porta 8080)
After=network.target

[Service]
User=yt-restapi
Group=yt-restapi
EnvironmentFile=/etc/yt-restapi.env
ExecStart=/usr/bin/python3 /usr/local/bin/bwb_status_monitor.py
Restart=always
RestartSec=3
# Nota: o monitor controla youtube-fallback via sudo; este serviço necessita
# de permitir a escalada pontual, caso contrário sudo falha com "no new
# privileges" e o fallback nunca arranca.
#NoNewPrivileges=true
PrivateTmp=true
ProtectSystem=full
ProtectHome=true
CapabilityBoundingSet=
AmbientCapabilities=

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target
-- youtube-fallback.service --
FragmentPath: /etc/systemd/system/youtube-fallback.service
FragmentTimestamp: <desconhecido>
$ systemctl cat youtube-fallback.service
(returncode=0)
stdout:
# /etc/systemd/system/youtube-fallback.service
[Unit]
Description=YouTube Secondary (Backup) - Slate 720p com imagem e textos
Wants=network-online.target
After=network-online.target
StartLimitIntervalSec=30
StartLimitBurst=10

[Service]
Type=simple
EnvironmentFile=/etc/youtube-fallback.env
ExecStart=/usr/local/bin/youtube_fallback.sh
Restart=always
RestartSec=3
Nice=5
LimitNOFILE=1048576

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target
